        "value":""

    },
    {
        "type":"comment",

    },

        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"    $ff = new Physics::Unit('furlong / fortnight', 'ff');"

        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"

    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"    print $ff->type, \"\\n\";         # prints:  Speed"

        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },

    {
        "type":"comment",

    {
        "type":"newline",

    },
    {
        "type":"comment",

        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"    # Get canonical string representation"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"    print $ff->expanded, \"\\n\";     # prints:  0.0001663... m s^-1"
    },

        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },

        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {

        "value":"\r\n"
    },

        "type":"comment",
        "value":"=head1 DESCRIPTION"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"These modules provide classes for the representation of physical units and"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"quantities, as well as a large library of predefined Physics::Unit objects."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"New units and quantities can be created with simple human-readable expressions"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"(for example, C<cubic meters per second>).  The resultant objects can then be"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"manipulated arithmetically, with the dimensionality correctly maintained."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"Physics::Unit objects generally represent standard, named units,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"like B<meter> or B<electronvolt>."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"L<Physics::Unit::Scalar|Physics::Unit::Scalar> and related classes, on the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"other hand, are used to represent various quantities that might occur as the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"result of a measurement or a specification, like \"5.7 meters\" or \"7.4"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"teraelectronvolts\"."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"A Physics::Unit object has a list of names, a dimensionality, and a magnitude."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"For example, the SI unit of force is the B<newton>.  In this module, it can be"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"referred to with any of the names B<newton>, B<nt>, or B<newtons>.  It's dimensionality"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"is that of a force:  mass X distance / time^2.  It's magnitude is 1000, which"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"expresses how large it is in terms of the unprefixed base units B<gram>, B<meter>, and B<second>."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"Units are created through the use of unit expressions, which allow"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"you to combine previously defined named units in new and interesting"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"ways. In the synopsis above, C<furlong / fortnight> is a unit"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"expression."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"Units that have the same dimensionality (for example, B<acres> and B<square kilometers>)"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"can be compared, and converted from one to the other."

    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"=head1 TYPES OF UNITS"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"A Unit can have one or more names associated with it, or it can be"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"unnamed (anonymous).  Named units are immutable. This ensures that"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"expressions used to derive other Units will remain consistent."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"The values of anonymous Unit objects, however, can change."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"Among named Units, there are three types: prefixes (for example,"
    },

        "value":""

        "value":"\r\n"

        "value":""

        "value":"\r\n"

        "value":""

        "type":"comment",

        "value":""

        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",

    },
    {

    {

        "value":""
    },

        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"=back"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",

    },
    {

    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"in a natural way.  For example, note that the space operator has higher precedence"

        "value":"\r\n"

    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"than '*', '/', or 'per'.  Thus \"C<meters/sec sec>\" is a unit of acceleration,"

    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"=head2 Expression Grammar"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"This is the approximate grammar used by the parser."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"  expr : term"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"       | term '/' expr"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"       | term '*' expr"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"       | term 'per' expr"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"  term : factor"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"       | term <whitespace> factor"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"  factor : primary"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"         | primary '**' integer"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"  primary : number"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | word"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | '(' expr ')'"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | 'square' primary"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | 'sq' primary"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | 'cubic' primary"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | primary 'squared'"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"          | primary 'cubed'"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"=head1 PREDEFINED UNIT LIBRARY"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"A rather complete set of units is pre-defined in the unit library, so it"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"will probably be rare that you'll need to define your own. See the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"L<UnitsByName|Physics::Unit::UnitsByName> or"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"L<UnitsByType|Physics::Unit::UnitsByType> page for a complete list."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"A B<pound> is a unit of force. I was very much tempted to make it a unit"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"of mass, since that is the way it is used in everyday speech, but I just"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"couldn't do it. The everyday pound, then, is named B<pound-mass>,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"B<lbm>, B<lbms>, or B<pounds-mass>."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":""
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"However, I couldn't bring myself to do the same thing to all the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"other American units derived from a B<pound>. Therefore, B<ounce>, B<ton>,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
